**Tercios**

*   [![Allowed tercio fraction.png](/images/thumb/5/53/Allowed_tercio_fraction.png/28px-Allowed_tercio_fraction.png)](/File:Allowed_tercio_fraction.png) **+15%** Tercio force limit fraction
*   [![Yearly army tradition.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Yearly_army_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_army_tradition.png)](/Yearly_army_tradition "Yearly army tradition") **+0.5** Yearly army tradition
*   [![Yearly army professionalism](/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Yearly army professionalism") **+0.25%** Yearly army professionalism

![Tercios icon](/images/thumb/b/b7/Gov_tercios_reform.png/40px-Gov_tercios_reform.png "Tercios icon")

The Tercios, literary 'A Third', were the backbone of the Spanish armies in the Early Modern Age. While historically the Tercios were not only drafted from Spain, but also from Italy or Wallonia, the most valuable Tercios were drafted from Spanish provinces. Tercios were almost unbeatable for decades in the battlefields across Europe and the Mediterranean, and were key to the evolution of European warfare.

**Conditions** :

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

Available only with the [Domination](/Domination "Domination") DLC enabled.

*   At least one of:
    *   All of:
        *   The country is _or_ was [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon")
        *   At least one of:
            *   Country's total [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") development is at least 500
            *   Is a [great power](/Great_power "Great power")
    *   Has completed the [![Flag of Castile](/images/thumb/e/ee/Castile.png/20px-Castile.png)](/Castile "Castile") Castilean [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") mission _“Assemble the Tercios”_
*   [![Piety](/images/thumb/8/8f/Monthly_piety.png/28px-Monthly_piety.png)](/Piety "Piety") Religion is **not** in Muslim group

* * *

**Additional effects** :

*   [![Amount of tercio.png](/images/thumb/5/53/Amount_of_tercio.png/28px-Amount_of_tercio.png)](/File:Amount_of_tercio.png) Country allows tercio infantry

Their light armor allows them to strike fast and retreat before the enemy is able to regroup. The almogavars have lost their power with the end of the Reconquista, but with new enemies on the horizon their skills are needed once again.

*   [![Vassal force limit contribution.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Vassal_force_limit_contribution.png/28px-Vassal_force_limit_contribution.png)](/Vassal_force_limit_contribution "Vassal force limit contribution") **+33%** Vassal force limit contribution

![Manrent icon](/images/thumb/f/ff/Gov_feudal_levies.png/40px-Gov_feudal_levies.png "Manrent icon")

The manrent is a contract between the chiefs of the clans and the ruling crown. In exchange for protection and privileges, the clans would pledge their loyalty to their ruler and serve them in their military.

**Conditions** :

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

Available only with the [Domination](/Domination "Domination") DLC enabled.

*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Primary culture is Scottish

  

**Merchant Arsenal**

*   [![Recover navy morale speed.png](/images/thumb/1/1c/Recover_navy_morale_speed.png/28px-Recover_navy_morale_speed.png)](/Recover_navy_morale_speed "Recover navy morale speed") **+20%** Recover navy morale speed
*   [![Shipbuilding time.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Shipbuilding_time.png/28px-Shipbuilding_time.png)](/Shipbuilding_time "Shipbuilding time") **−25%** Shipbuilding time

![Merchant Arsenal icon](/images/thumb/f/f4/Gov_merchant_ship.png/40px-Gov_merchant_ship.png "Merchant Arsenal icon")

While our state is primarily focused on profit and trade, it is undeniable that these interests need to be protected through military means. The arsenal of the state is prepared for military conflicts as it houses galleasses and other weapons of war.

**Conditions** :

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

Available only with the [Domination](/Domination "Domination") DLC enabled.

*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture is Venetian or Ligurian

* * *

**Additional effects** :

*   [![Has galleass.png](/images/thumb/2/2b/Has_galleass.png/28px-Has_galleass.png)](/File:Has_galleass.png) Country allows galleass ships

  

**Allotment System**

*   [![Manpower in own culture provinces.png](/images/thumb/1/14/Manpower_in_own_culture_provinces.png/28px-Manpower_in_own_culture_provinces.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") **+33%** Manpower in primary culture provinces
*   [![Manpower in accepted culture provinces.png](/images/thumb/7/73/Manpower_in_accepted_culture_provinces.png/28px-Manpower_in_accepted_culture_provinces.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") **+20%** Manpower in accepted culture provinces
*   [![Manpower in same culture group provinces.png](/images/thumb/2/26/Manpower_in_same_culture_group_provinces.png/28px-Manpower_in_same_culture_group_provinces.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") **+10%** Manpower in same culture group provinces

![Allotment System icon](/images/thumb/a/ad/Gov_allotment_system.png/40px-Gov_allotment_system.png "Allotment System icon")

The Allotment System ("Indelningsverket") is a organization system for the military which enables the quick mobilization of the country. Every tenth man between the age of 15 and 44 will be conscripted as permanent part of the national infantry while the Nobility, exempted from their taxes, have to provide with their cavalry.

**Conditions:**

*   Has completed the [![Flag of Sweden](/images/thumb/9/98/Sweden.png/20px-Sweden.png)](/Sweden "Sweden") Swedish [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions")"Reform the Military" mission

* * *

**Additional effects:**

[![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North")

Available only with the [Lions of the North](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North") DLC enabled.

*   [![Has carolean.png](/images/thumb/8/83/Has_carolean.png/28px-Has_carolean.png)](/File:Has_carolean.png) Allows Recruitment of Carolean units

  

**Expanded Black Army**

*   [![War taxes cost](/images/thumb/8/8a/War_taxes_cost.png/28px-War_taxes_cost.png)](/War_taxes "War taxes cost") **−50%** War taxes cost
*   [![Mercenary manpower.png](/images/thumb/b/b2/Mercenary_manpower.png/28px-Mercenary_manpower.png)](/Mercenary_manpower "Mercenary manpower") **+100%** mercenary manpower
*   [![Army tradition from battles](/images/thumb/a/ae/Prestige_from_land_battles.png/28px-Prestige_from_land_battles.png)](/Army_tradition "Army tradition from battles") **+100%** army tradition from battles

![Expanded Black Army icon](/images/thumb/0/0b/Black_army_reform.png/40px-Black_army_reform.png "Expanded Black Army icon")

The need for a professional army to guard our tumultuous borders has given rise to voices across our court, demanding the expansion of the privileges surrounding the Black Army, a powerful mercenary army, equipped with excellent steel and devoted to the arts of warfare.

**Conditions:**

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

### Separation of Power\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=12 "Edit section: Separation of Power") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=12 "Edit section: Separation of Power")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Seize Executive Power**

*   Changes government type to [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Monarchy.
*   Lose **\-3** [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") Stability

![Seize Executive Power icon](/images/thumb/9/98/King_2_highlighted.png/40px-King_2_highlighted.png "Seize Executive Power icon")

Republicanism has served us well but it is time we empower a strong ruler to take our state into a new era.

**Proclaim Divine Guidance**

*   Changes government type to[![Government theocracy.png](/images/thumb/8/81/Government_theocracy.png/28px-Government_theocracy.png)](/Theocracy "Theocracy")Theocracy.
*   Lose **\-3** [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") Stability

![Proclaim Divine Guidance icon](/images/thumb/5/54/Religious_leader_highlighted.png/40px-Religious_leader_highlighted.png "Proclaim Divine Guidance icon")

Divine guidance and not popular support must be the governing rule in our state. Let us appoint someone who will truly care for the moral well-being of our subjects.

  

**Parliamentarism**

*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** National unrest

![Parliamentarism icon](/images/thumb/9/99/Gov_judge.png/40px-Gov_judge.png "Parliamentarism icon")

It is time we separate the head of government from the head of state and give the legislative assemblies of the land a larger share in the day to day rule of our state.

**Conditions:**

*   the country does _not_ have the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estate **or**
    *   the crown owns more land than the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estate **and**
    *   the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estates loyalty is higher than their influence.
*   the country is _not_ the “[Celestial Empire](/Celestial_Empire "Celestial Empire")”, [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") Revolutionary or [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") Piratical
*   Not available with certain unique reforms

* * *

**Additional effects:**

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")

Available only with the [Common Sense](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") DLC enabled.

*   Enables [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") [parliament](/Parliament "Parliament")
*   Disables the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility") nobility estate
*   Disables “[Call diet](/Call_diet "Call diet")”

  

**Presidential System**

*   [![Institution embracement cost.png](/images/thumb/e/e6/Institution_embracement_cost.png/28px-Institution_embracement_cost.png)](/Embracement_cost "Embracement cost") **−10%** Institution embracement cost
*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism") **+5** Maximum absolutism

![Presidential System icon](/images/thumb/c/c5/Gov_man_on_podium.png/40px-Gov_man_on_podium.png "Presidential System icon")

The Chairman or President of our governing body must be elected separately from the legislative branch of government. The president can then appoint or dismiss members of the government.

**Supremacy of the Diet**

*   [![All estates' loyalty equilibrium.png](/images/thumb/3/3c/All_estates%27_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-All_estates%27_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/All_estates_loyalty_equilibrium "All estates loyalty equilibrium") **+10%** All estates' loyalty equilibrium
*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism") **−25** Maximum absolutism

![Supremacy of the Diet icon](/images/thumb/0/07/Gov_council.png/40px-Gov_council.png "Supremacy of the Diet icon")

Our president rules the country, but the power of the jurisdiction and the executive lies in the hands of the estates. As such, the diet has been strengthened in their role to govern the many aspects of the republic.

**Conditions:**

*   Has any estates
*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") Pirate Republic

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   Calling the Diet no longer increases [![Estate influence](/images/9/98/Estates_influence.png)](/Estates "Estate influence") Influence
*   Elections raise the [![Estate influence](/images/9/98/Estates_influence.png)](/Estates "Estate influence") Influece of the Candidates Estate
*   Calling the Diet increases [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") Republican Tradition by **0.5**, multiplied by the Length of your Election Term

**Attorney General**

*   [![Cost of advisors with ruler's culture](/images/thumb/9/9c/Cost_of_advisors_with_ruler%27s_culture.png/28px-Cost_of_advisors_with_ruler%27s_culture.png)](/Advisor_costs "Cost of advisors with ruler's culture") **−15%** Cost of advisors with ruler's culture

![Attorney General icon](/images/thumb/c/cb/Reform_three_classes.png/40px-Reform_three_classes.png "Attorney General icon")

The attorney general is the main legal advisor to our government, and has the responsibility of the jurisdiction of our country. This separation of power ensures the safety of our population and an easier integration of newly annexed subjects.

**Additional Effects:**

*   [![Advisor.png](/images/thumb/6/6a/Advisor.png/28px-Advisor.png)](/Advisor "Advisor")Advisors increase [![Yearly republican tradition.png](/images/thumb/6/68/Yearly_republican_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_republican_tradition.png)](/Yearly_republican_tradition "Yearly republican tradition") yearly Republican Tradition by **0.02** times their Level
*   Can not [![Crownland.png](/images/thumb/e/ed/Crownland.png/28px-Crownland.png)](/Crown_land "Crown land") seize Crownland

**A Revolutionary Empire**

*   Changes government type to [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Monarchy.
*   Enact tier 1 reform [Revolutionary Empire](/Revolutionary_Empire "Revolutionary Empire")

![A Revolutionary Empire icon](/images/thumb/8/88/Reform_become_rev_empire.png/40px-Reform_become_rev_empire.png "A Revolutionary Empire icon")

Even in a Republic fueled by the fires of Revolution, it’s becoming clear that political dynasties are being established in our nation. Our President wishes to crown himself Emperor and continue to spread the ideals of the Revolution, with the Emperorship claiming sovereignty over all people.

**Conditions:**

*   Only available for [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") ‘Revolutionary Republic’
*   If the [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") [Rights of Man](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") DLC is active:
    *   [![Imperial influence](/images/thumb/5/5b/Imperial_influence.png/28px-Imperial_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Imperial influence") The imperialists must have at least 75 influence
*   else:
    *   [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") republican tradition must be below **40**

  

**The Feuillant System**

*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **−10%** Stability cost modifier
*   [![Yearly republican tradition.png](/images/thumb/6/68/Yearly_republican_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_republican_tradition.png)](/Yearly_republican_tradition "Yearly republican tradition") **−0.1** Yearly republican tradition

![The Feuillant System icon](/images/thumb/4/49/Reform_feuillant.png/40px-Reform_feuillant.png "The Feuillant System icon")

There are many citizens and politicians in the Republic who wish to return to the tyranny of an absolute monarchy. However, the Feuillant political group believe in a compromise; that powers in the nation should be split between an Emperor and a President, similar to a constitutional monarchy. By riding the delicate balance between Empire and Republic, we may actually please both the Imperialists and Republicans within our nation.

**Conditions:**

**The Two-Chamber System**

*   [![Free policies.png](/images/thumb/7/79/Free_policies.png/28px-Free_policies.png)](/Free_policies "Free policies") **+1** Free policies
*   [![Yearly republican tradition.png](/images/thumb/6/68/Yearly_republican_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_republican_tradition.png)](/Yearly_republican_tradition "Yearly republican tradition") **+0.15** Yearly republican tradition

![The Two-Chamber System icon](/images/thumb/b/b6/Gov_parliament_hall.png/40px-Gov_parliament_hall.png "The Two-Chamber System icon")

For a long time, the Canton system maintained the peace, stability, and independence of small democratic leagues like the Swiss and Swabian Federations. By similarly dividing our legislature into a Grand Council representing the Cantons, and the Senate representing the republic as a whole, we may protect the interests of the individual cities and cultural identities within our nation while still placing the values of the Revolution above all else!

*   Ruler stats depend on [![Admiral.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Admiral.png/28px-Admiral.png)](/Admiral "Admiral") admiral pips. On average 12 ruler points for 16-pips admiral.

The pirates that run amok in the Republic cannot be trusted to bathe themselves, let alone to govern a nation whose future hands on the edge of a cutlass. A Consortium formed of the most influential black market merchants shall be established as its true governors. Profit must come before liberty.

Trade company governing cost

*   [![Goods produced modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Goods_produced_modifier.png/28px-Goods_produced_modifier.png)](/Goods_produced_modifier "Goods produced modifier") Bonus goods production in provinces not owned by merchant republics or trade companies, proportional to percentage of trade power in the node (e.g., non-owned provinces produce 50% bonus goods if the republic controls 100% of trade in the node).
*   AI is more reluctant to be diplomatically vassalized by or as a merchant republic (**−10** reasons if the proposer is and **−30** reasons if the target is).

*   Vassals, marches, and client states, which usually do not transfer [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power") [trade power](/Trade_power "Trade power") to their overlord, will transfer **50%** if the overlord is a merchant republic.

**Imperial Diplomacy**

*   [![Diplomatic reputation.png](/images/thumb/2/21/Diplomatic_reputation.png/28px-Diplomatic_reputation.png)](/Diplomatic_reputation "Diplomatic reputation") **+2** Diplomatic reputation
*   [![Diplomatic relations.png](/images/thumb/5/58/Diplomatic_relations.png/28px-Diplomatic_relations.png)](/Diplomatic_relations "Diplomatic relations") **+1** Diplomatic relations

![Imperial Diplomacy icon](/images/thumb/4/49/Gov_king.png/40px-Gov_king.png "Imperial Diplomacy icon")

The city cannot maintain its independence without the support of the Emperor and our other allies. We shall focus our energies on strengthening our diplomatic ties and ensuring that, whenever we have need of them, our friends will be there to help us defend the city.

**Conditions:**

*   Is ‘Free city’

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   The [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") emperor gains the _Imperial Diplomacy_ opinion modifier towards this country giving [![Icon diplomacy relations.png](/images/e/e6/Icon_diplomacy_relations.png)](/Relations "Relations") **+50** relations

**Municipal Self-Defense**

*   [![Manpower.png](/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") **+5000** Manpower increase
*   [![Land force limit modifier.png](/images/thumb/8/85/Land_force_limit_modifier.png/28px-Land_force_limit_modifier.png)](/Land_force_limit_modifier "Land force limit modifier") **+25%** Land force limit modifier

![Municipal Self-Defense icon](/images/thumb/8/8a/Gov_soldiers_7.png/40px-Gov_soldiers_7.png "Municipal Self-Defense icon")

Only by relying on the military capabilities of our city can we ensure our survival. We shall allocate more political power to the captains of the City Watch and ensure that they have all they need to provide for our defense.

**Conditions:**

*   Is ‘Free city’

  

**Governing Senate**

*   [![All estates' loyalty equilibrium.png](/images/thumb/3/3c/All_estates%27_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-All_estates%27_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/All_estates_loyalty_equilibrium "All estates loyalty equilibrium") **+10%** All estates' loyalty equilibrium
*   [![All estates influence](/images/thumb/d/d4/All_estate_influence_modifier.png/28px-All_estate_influence_modifier.png)](/Estates "All estates influence") **−10%** All estates influence modifier
*   [![All estates possible privileges](/images/thumb/c/c6/All_estate_possible_privileges.png/28px-All_estate_possible_privileges.png)](/Estates "All estates possible privileges") **+1** Max privileges per estate

![Governing Senate icon](/images/thumb/1/18/Gov_governing_senate.png/40px-Gov_governing_senate.png "Governing Senate icon")

The governing senate is the assembly of our ruler's most trusted advisors and the highest legislative, judicial and executive institution of the empire. Unlike its predecessor, the boyar Duma, the senate covers the concerns of all the estates and senators.

**Conditions** :

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

Available only with the [Domination](/Domination "Domination") DLC enabled.

*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary
*   Is _not_ [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") a Pirate Republic
*   At least one of:
    *   Was unlocked via the [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") Russian [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") mission "The governing Senate"
    *   Has enacted the _“Ruthenian Tsardom”_ government reform
*   If DLC [![Res Publica.png](/images/thumb/b/b5/Res_Publica.png/28px-Res_Publica.png)](/Res_Publica "Res Publica") Res Publica is active :
    *   Has _not_ enacted the _“Elective Monarchy”_ government reform
*   If DLC [![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North") Lions of the North is active :
    *   Has _not_ enacted the _“Polish Elective Monarchy”_ government reform
*   If DLC [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven") Mandate of Heaven is active :
    *   Has _not_ enacted the _“Celestial Empire”_ government reform

* * *

**Additional effects :**

*   Calling the diet no longer raises [![All estates influence](/images/thumb/d/d4/All_estate_influence_modifier.png/28px-All_estate_influence_modifier.png)](/Estates "All estates influence") estate influence

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

*   Has access to [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament

  

**Enforced Autocracy**

*   [![Culture conversion cost.png](/images/thumb/5/5e/Culture_conversion_cost.png/28px-Culture_conversion_cost.png)](/Culture_conversion_cost "Culture conversion cost") **−20%** Culture conversion time
*   [![Yearly government power.png](/images/thumb/b/b8/Yearly_government_power.png/28px-Yearly_government_power.png)](/File:Yearly_government_power.png)**+0.5** Yearly government power

![Enforced Autocracy icon](/images/thumb/d/d7/Gov_russian_queen.png/40px-Gov_russian_queen.png "Enforced Autocracy icon")

The rule of the Emperor is absolute and can not be second to anyone. The estates and other institutions of the state are bound to the Emperor.

**Conditions** :

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

### Regionalism\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=13 "Edit section: Regionalism") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=13 "Edit section: Regionalism")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Provincial Governments**

*   [![State maintenance.png](/images/thumb/1/1c/State_maintenance.png/28px-State_maintenance.png)](/State_maintenance "State maintenance") **−25%** State maintenance
*   [![Global prosperity growth.png](/images/thumb/f/f4/Global_prosperity_growth.png/28px-Global_prosperity_growth.png)](/Global_prosperity_growth "Global prosperity growth") **+0.50** Global prosperity growth

![Provincial Governments icon](/images/thumb/5/51/Gov_landscape.png/40px-Gov_landscape.png "Provincial Governments icon")

In order for our administration to be efficient we must allow provincial governments the freedom they need to perform their functions. Local elections will ensure that trustworthy individuals can be appointed who would then answer to the central government.

**Administrative Divisions**

*   [![Governing capacity.png](/images/thumb/2/2b/Governing_capacity.png/28px-Governing_capacity.png)](/Governing_capacity "Governing capacity") **+250** Governing capacity

![Administrative Divisions icon](/images/thumb/6/6b/Gov_map.png/40px-Gov_map.png "Administrative Divisions icon")

Let us divide the state into geographic regions ruled and administered by officials appointed by our central government.

**Union of States**

*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Global_trade_power "Global trade power") **+10%** Global trade power

![Union of States icon](/images/thumb/f/f4/Gov_merchant_ship.png/40px-Gov_merchant_ship.png "Union of States icon")

Rather than one unified state our country has grown from a large number of states integrated into one confederacy. As our administration grows and evolves we must not infringe on the rights of the member states, doing so would trample on the very principles of our existence.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") Pirate Republic

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   Has merchant republic mechanics:

State governing cost

Trade company governing cost

*   [![Goods produced modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Goods_produced_modifier.png/28px-Goods_produced_modifier.png)](/Goods_produced_modifier "Goods produced modifier") Bonus goods production in provinces not owned by merchant republics or trade companies, proportional to percentage of trade power in the node (e.g., non-owned provinces produce 50% bonus goods if the republic controls 100% of trade in the node).
*   AI is more reluctant to be diplomatically vassalized by or as a merchant republic (**−10** reasons if the proposer is and **−30** reasons if the target is).

[![Wealth of Nations.png](/images/thumb/7/7d/Wealth_of_Nations.png/28px-Wealth_of_Nations.png)](/Wealth_of_Nations "Wealth of Nations")

*   Vassals, marches, and client states, which usually do not transfer [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power") [trade power](/Trade_power "Trade power") to their overlord, will transfer **50%** if the overlord is a merchant republic.

[![Res Publica.png](/images/thumb/b/b5/Res_Publica.png/28px-Res_Publica.png)](/Res_Publica "Res Publica")

Available only with the [Res Publica](/Res_Publica "Res Publica") DLC enabled.

*   Can construct a trade post for [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** administrative power, giving [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power") **+10** trade power, in one owned province per trade node (except the node containing the main trade city).

**Cultural Administration**

*   [![Max promoted cultures.png](/images/thumb/8/8b/Max_promoted_cultures.png/28px-Max_promoted_cultures.png)](/Max_promoted_cultures "Max promoted cultures") **+2** Max promoted cultures
*   [![Promote culture cost.png](/images/thumb/7/76/Promote_culture_cost.png/28px-Promote_culture_cost.png)](/Promote_culture_cost "Promote culture cost") **−50%** Promote culture cost

![Cultural Administration icon](/images/thumb/e/ee/Reform_conciliarism.png/40px-Reform_conciliarism.png "Cultural Administration icon")

Our nation is home to many different cultures foreign to our own. In order to reduce tensions within our country the state is divided by the different cultures, and each culture elects their representative to administrate them.

  

**Exile Colonial Companies**

*   [![Expel minorities cost.png](/images/thumb/d/d4/Expel_minorities_cost.png/28px-Expel_minorities_cost.png)](/Expel_minorities_cost "Expel minorities cost") **−100%** Expel minorities cost
*   [![Settler chance.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Settler_chance.png/28px-Settler_chance.png)](/Settler_chance "Settler chance")**+5%** Settler Chance

![Exile Colonial Companies icon](/images/thumb/f/f4/Gov_merchant_ship.png/40px-Gov_merchant_ship.png "Exile Colonial Companies icon")

The New World is a place of great opportunity, and for us it is an opportunity to establish Exile Colonies and rid our nation of convicts and minorities. By allowing colonial companies to claim sovereignty over our undesirables, we will create harmony in the Old World and expand our influence in the New World.

**Conditions:**

[![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century")

Available only with the [Golden Century](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") DLC enabled.

*   Country has capital in Africa, Asia or Europe
*   Has [![Exploration idea group.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Exploration_idea_group.png/28px-Exploration_idea_group.png)](/Exploration_ideas "Exploration ideas") Exploration Ideas

  

### Economical Matters\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=14 "Edit section: Economical Matters") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=14 "Edit section: Economical Matters")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

  

**Empower the Burghers**

*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Global_trade_power "Global trade power") **+5%** Global trade power
*   [![Trade efficiency.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Trade_efficiency.png/28px-Trade_efficiency.png)](/Trade_efficiency "Trade efficiency") **+5%** Trade efficiency
*   [![Burghers loyalty equilibrium.png](/images/thumb/e/e5/Burghers_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-Burghers_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/Burghers_loyalty_equilibrium "Burghers loyalty equilibrium")/ [![Vaishyas.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Vaishyas.png/28px-Vaishyas.png)](/Vaishyas "Vaishyas") **+5%** Burghers/ Vaishyas loyalty equilibrium
*   [![Burghers influence.png](/images/thumb/0/0d/Burghers_influence.png/28px-Burghers_influence.png)](/Burghers_influence "Burghers influence")/ [![Jains.png](/images/thumb/9/95/Jains.png/28px-Jains.png)](/Jains "Jains") / [![Vaishyas.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Vaishyas.png/28px-Vaishyas.png)](/Vaishyas "Vaishyas")**+10%** Burghers/ Jains/ Vaishyas influence

![Empower the Burghers icon](/images/thumb/8/8b/Gov_prussian_monarchy_2.png/40px-Gov_prussian_monarchy_2.png "Empower the Burghers icon")

The Burghers are the traders and merchants of our state. They ensure that a constant stream of money finds its way into our state. To empower their privileges and their influence leads to a faster accumulation of our wealth.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’
*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary

  

**Curtail the Burghers**

*   [![Trade company governing cost.png](/images/thumb/6/6a/Trade_company_governing_cost.png/28px-Trade_company_governing_cost.png)](/Governing_capacity "Governing capacity") **−10%** Trade company governing cost
*   [![Trade steering.png](/images/thumb/b/b1/Trade_steering.png/28px-Trade_steering.png)](/Trade_steering "Trade steering") **+15%** Trade steering
*   [![Burghers influence.png](/images/thumb/0/0d/Burghers_influence.png/28px-Burghers_influence.png)](/Burghers_influence "Burghers influence") **\-10%** Burghers influence

![Curtail the Burghers icon](/images/thumb/4/47/Gov_assembly_hall.png/40px-Gov_assembly_hall.png "Curtail the Burghers icon")

The rights and privileges of the Burghers have been too vast for far too long. Wars and expansion of the state are confronted by a lack of support from our own class of merchants. It is time to curtail the rights of the traders and create a centralized state.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’
*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary

* * *

**Additional effects:**

*   Seizing Land from [![Burghers.png](/images/thumb/d/dd/Burghers.png/28px-Burghers.png)](/Burghers "Burghers")Burghers no longer triggers [![Particularist rebels.png](/images/thumb/8/85/Particularist_rebels.png/24px-Particularist_rebels.png)](/Particularists "Particularists")Revolts

  

**Mercantilistic Approach**

*   [![Cost to promote mercantilism.png](/images/thumb/c/c1/Cost_to_promote_mercantilism.png/28px-Cost_to_promote_mercantilism.png)](/Cost_to_promote_mercantilism "Cost to promote mercantilism") **−10%** Cost to promote mercantilism
*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Domestic_trade_power "Domestic trade power") **+15%** Domestic trade power
*   [![Merchant trade power.png](/images/thumb/3/39/Merchant_trade_power.png/28px-Merchant_trade_power.png)](/Merchant_trade_power "Merchant trade power") **+5** Merchant trade power

![Mercantilistic Approach icon](/images/thumb/9/93/Gov_paper_with_seal.png/40px-Gov_paper_with_seal.png "Mercantilistic Approach icon")

Free trade implies an equal relation between imports and exports of goods. While beneficial for certain goods, it is of little value for our state. Only through maximizing our exports while minimizing the import from foreign powers, our state can grow its economy.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

* * *

**Additional effects:**

*   The Privilege "Indepted to the Burghers" no longer lowers [![Mercantilism.png](/images/thumb/0/05/Mercantilism.png/28px-Mercantilism.png)](/Mercantilism "Mercantilism")Mercantilism

  

**Embrace Free Trade**

*   [![Institution spread.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Institution_spread.png/28px-Institution_spread.png)](/Institution_spread "Institution spread") **+25%** Institution spread
*   [![Trade power abroad.png](/images/thumb/a/a9/Trade_power_abroad.png/28px-Trade_power_abroad.png)](/Trade_power_abroad "Trade power abroad") **+20%** Trade power abroad

![Embrace Free Trade icon](/images/thumb/8/8f/Gov_merchant.png/40px-Gov_merchant.png "Embrace Free Trade icon")

Merchants from all of the world should be able to travel into our lands to engage with our population in trade and commerce. Abandoning the narrowness of mercantalism, the state gains an easier access to foreign thoughts.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

* * *

**Additional effects:**

*   Gain [![All power costs.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/All_power_costs.png/28px-All_power_costs.png)](/Monarch_power "Monarch power")**100** of every Monarch Power when [![Institutions.png](/images/thumb/4/43/Institutions.png/28px-Institutions.png)](/Institutions "Institutions") embracing an Institution

[![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")

Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") DLC enabled.

*   The Trading Policy "Improve Inland Routes" no longer requires [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power")Trade Power

  

**Embrace the Economic Theory**

*   [![Interest per annum.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Interest_per_annum.png/28px-Interest_per_annum.png)](/Interest_per_annum "Interest per annum") **\-0.5** Interest per Annum
*   [![Yearly inflation reduction.png](/images/thumb/7/79/Yearly_inflation_reduction.png/28px-Yearly_inflation_reduction.png)](/Inflation_reduction "Inflation reduction") **+0.2** Yearly inflation reduction

![Embrace the Economic Theory icon](/images/thumb/8/8a/Gov_dutch_flag.png/40px-Gov_dutch_flag.png "Embrace the Economic Theory icon")

The economy plays an undeniably important role within the apparatus of the state. The complex systems of trade, finance and luxury need to be tamed to serve the health of the government.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

  

**Lockean Proviso**

*   [![Development cost.png](/images/thumb/a/a2/Development_cost.png/28px-Development_cost.png)](/Development_cost "Development cost") **−5%** Development cost
*   [![Goods produced modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Goods_produced_modifier.png/28px-Goods_produced_modifier.png)](/Goods_produced_modifier "Goods produced modifier") **+5%** Goods produced modifier

![Lockean Proviso icon](/images/thumb/e/e8/Gov_paper_money_map.png/40px-Gov_paper_money_map.png "Lockean Proviso icon")

Unused property is a waste to both nature and the state. By introducing and emphasizing hard goods which yield utility over periods of time, the people can exchange their exessive possessions without offending the natural law. The government would moderate the conflict between accumulation of property and distribution of wealth.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’
*   Has completed [![Economic idea group.png](/images/thumb/9/9d/Economic_idea_group.png/28px-Economic_idea_group.png)](/Economic_ideas "Economic ideas") Economic Ideas or [![Infrastructure idea group.png](/images/thumb/b/b3/Infrastructure_idea_group.png/28px-Infrastructure_idea_group.png)](/Infrastructure_ideas "Infrastructure ideas") Infrastructure Ideas

  

**War Economy**

*   [![War taxes cost](/images/thumb/8/8a/War_taxes_cost.png/28px-War_taxes_cost.png)](/War_taxes "War taxes cost") **−50%** War taxes cost
*   [![Regiment cost.png](/images/thumb/2/2e/Regiment_cost.png/28px-Regiment_cost.png)](/Regiment_cost "Regiment cost") **−10%** Regiment cost
*   [![Ship costs.png](/images/thumb/d/d2/Ship_costs.png/28px-Ship_costs.png)](/Ship_cost "Ship cost") **−10%** Ship cost

![War Economy icon](/images/thumb/1/16/Gov_war_economy.png/40px-Gov_war_economy.png "War Economy icon")

The economical security of the state is based on our ability to wage and win wars. Manufactories in our state have no other purpose than fueling our military ambitions.

**Conditions** :

*   Is _not_ [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") a Pirate Republic

  

**Exploitation of the New World**

*   [![Colonists.png](/images/thumb/3/34/Colonists.png/28px-Colonists.png)](/Colonist "Colonist") **+1** Colonists

![Exploitation of the New World icon](/images/thumb/6/62/Gov_compass.png/40px-Gov_compass.png "Exploitation of the New World icon")

The resources of the New World are plenty and of great value. By granting certain rights and privileges to our merchants, we can assure that these foreign goods are exploited and transported to our state, which we then distribute in the Old World.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’
*   Capital is NOT in a Colonial Region

**Additional effects:**

*   Colonial Subjects gain a **+10%** [![Goods produced modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Goods_produced_modifier.png/28px-Goods_produced_modifier.png)](/Goods_produced_modifier "Goods produced modifier")Goods Produced Modifier

  

**Thalassocracy**

*   [![Center of trade upgrade cost.png](/images/thumb/6/65/Center_of_trade_upgrade_cost.png/28px-Center_of_trade_upgrade_cost.png)](/Center_of_trade_upgrade_cost "Center of trade upgrade cost") **−10%** Center of trade upgrade cost
*   [![Trade company investment cost](/images/thumb/0/0d/Trade_company_investment_cost.png/28px-Trade_company_investment_cost.png)](/Trade_company_investment "Trade company investment cost") **−10%** Trade company investment cost
*   [![Naval forcelimit.png](/images/thumb/9/98/Naval_forcelimit.png/28px-Naval_forcelimit.png)](/Naval_forcelimit "Naval forcelimit") **+25%** Naval forcelimit modifier
*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Global_trade_power "Global trade power") **+15%** Global trade power

![Thalassocracy icon](/images/thumb/0/01/Reform_admiralty.png/40px-Reform_admiralty.png "Thalassocracy icon")

Thalassocracy, Rule by The Sea. Ours is a people whose lives are lived out with, by and for the sea. Our empire stretches far beyond our homeland and into far-flung colonies in our extended Outremer, our Lands Beyond The Sea. From coast to coasts beyond, our flags wave from ships upon the briny foam. The sea is cold, yet we have made it our home. Let no one challenge us in our proper element.

**Conditions** :

*   Unlocked by taking the [![Decision.png](/images/thumb/b/b1/Decision.png/28px-Decision.png)](/Decision "Decision") [Confirm Thalassocracy](/Confirm_Thalassocracy "Confirm Thalassocracy") decision

* * *

Vodka is a traditional alcoholic beverage for our people. By assuming direct control over its production and ensuring a monopoly of the liquor, we can also safeguard our control over the masses with cheap vodka.

We are pirates who enjoy raiding merchant ships and razing entire harbors. But we are also craftsmen who had to repair their own ships on more than one occasion in the past. We should offer our knowledge of ship building and repairing to the merchants who are not good targets for our usual privateering.

Opening trade with actual countries, which have laws and rules, is nearly impossible. However, trading with some of their rich citizens is a different story.\\nThe Smugglers have personal connections with a few rich mercenary company leaders who are more than willing to support us in exchange for some of our... legally acquired wares.

**Empower the Quartermasters**

*   [![Naval maintenance modifier.png](/images/thumb/3/32/Naval_maintenance_modifier.png/28px-Naval_maintenance_modifier.png)](/Naval_maintenance_modifier "Naval maintenance modifier") **−15%** Naval maintenance modifier

![Empower the Quartermasters icon](/images/thumb/8/8f/Gov_merchant.png/40px-Gov_merchant.png "Empower the Quartermasters icon")

While the Captains lead the crew, the Buccaneers fight and the Smugglers trade, it is the Quartermasters who keep the piratical business running. They are the ones who organize the rations, plan the raids and design the Pirate Code.\\nIn order for our confederation to run smoothly it is only logical to empower the Quartermasters.

**Conditions:**

*   Is [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

### Consolidation of Power\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=15 "Edit section: Consolidation of Power") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=15 "Edit section: Consolidation of Power")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Broaden Executive Powers**

*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost "Stability cost") **−15%** Stability cost modifier
*   [![All power costs.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/All_power_costs.png/28px-All_power_costs.png)](/All_power_costs "All power costs") **−2%** All power costs

![Broaden Executive Powers icon](/images/thumb/5/50/Gov_castle.png/40px-Gov_castle.png "Broaden Executive Powers icon")

As the country grows so does the need to be able to act swiftly and efficiently. The only way to ensure this is by broadening the powers of the executive branch so that it has the tools it needs.

**Devolution of Powers**

*   [![Advisor.png](/images/thumb/6/6a/Advisor.png/28px-Advisor.png)](/Advisor "Advisor") **+2** Possible Advisors
*   [![Autonomy.png](/images/thumb/a/a9/Autonomy.png/28px-Autonomy.png)](/Autonomy "Autonomy") **\-0.05** Monthly Autonomy Change

![Devolution of Powers icon](/images/thumb/9/96/Gov_generic_people.png/40px-Gov_generic_people.png "Devolution of Powers icon")

No single person can rule a country as big and complex as ours. Collecting such powers in the hand of one ruler is also contrary to the Republican ideals of our ancestors. Decentralization and Devolution is how we can best remain able to dynamically meet the needs of an ever-growing state.

**Consolidated Power**

*   [![Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/c/c2/Absolutism.png/28px-Absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Absolutism") **+2** Yearly absolutism
*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism") **+25** Maximum absolutism
*   [![Reelection cost.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Reelection_cost.png/28px-Reelection_cost.png)](/Reelection_cost "Reelection cost") **−10%** Reelection cost

![Consolidated Power icon](/images/thumb/1/1e/Gov_nobleman.png/40px-Gov_nobleman.png "Consolidated Power icon")

Some might consider this practice as anti-republican, but it is apparent that absolute rule has its benefits. By consolidating all the power under our ruler we can ensure that our country can keep pace with the absolute monarchies around us.

**Conditions:**

*   Does not have "Venetian Government" enacted
*   Is not Revolutionary
*   Is not a Pirate republic

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   Loose **\-60** [![Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/c/c2/Absolutism.png/28px-Absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Absolutism") Absolutism when electing a new Ruler
*   On Reelection gain **+10** [![Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/c/c2/Absolutism.png/28px-Absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Absolutism") Absolutism, multiplied by the Number of times this Ruler was reelected

**New Men**

*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism") **−20** Maximum absolutism
*   [![Length of election term.png](/images/thumb/b/b6/Length_of_election_term.png/28px-Length_of_election_term.png)](/Length_of_election_term "Length of election term") **\-1** Length of election term
*   [![Random candidate bonus.png](/images/thumb/2/28/Random_candidate_bonus.png/28px-Random_candidate_bonus.png)](/Random_candidate_bonus "Random candidate bonus") **+1** Random candidate bonus

![New Men icon](/images/thumb/7/7a/Gov_dutch_republic.png/40px-Gov_dutch_republic.png "New Men icon")

Our Republic can't trust those staying too long in power. We prefer to elect new men which have not been meddled in corruption and shady business.

**Conditions:**

*   Ruler must NOT rule for life
*   Is not a Pirate Republic

**Absolute Power of the President**

*   [![All power costs.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/All_power_costs.png/28px-All_power_costs.png)](/All_power_costs "All power costs") **−5%** All power costs
*   [![Length of election term.png](/images/thumb/b/b6/Length_of_election_term.png/28px-Length_of_election_term.png)](/Length_of_election_term "Length of election term") **+1** Length of election term

![Absolute Power of the President icon](/images/thumb/4/49/Gov_king.png/40px-Gov_king.png "Absolute Power of the President icon")

While we have members of our nation elected to represent the people of their constituency, we must never forget that it is the President who has been elected to represent all people. The role of the elected representatives within the Revolution should be merely to advise the President who wields absolute power over the Republic.

**Conditions:**

*   Only available for [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary countries with the [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

**A Revolutionary Council**

*   [![Maximum revolutionary zeal](/images/thumb/5/59/Maximum_revolutionary_zeal.png/28px-Maximum_revolutionary_zeal.png)](/Revolutionary_zeal "Maximum revolutionary zeal") **+10** Maximum revolutionary zeal
*   [![Length of election term.png](/images/thumb/b/b6/Length_of_election_term.png/28px-Length_of_election_term.png)](/Length_of_election_term "Length of election term") **−1** Length of election term

![A Revolutionary Council icon](/images/thumb/a/ac/Reform_revolutionary_council.png/40px-Reform_revolutionary_council.png "A Revolutionary Council icon")

It’s become clear that the cult of personality surrounding our ruler is rapidly returning us to the old ways of government. We cannot allow this to happen, so by concentrating power into a council of elected individuals to represent the values of the Revolution, we strip power away from the individual at our state’s head and create another shield against the horror of absolute rulership.

**Conditions:**

*   Only available for [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary countries with the [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

**Additional Effects:**

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")

Available only with the [Common Sense](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") DLC enabled.

*   Has access to [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament

**Expand Buccaneers' Power**

*   [![Buccaneers influence](/images/thumb/5/5d/Buccaneers_influence.png/28px-Buccaneers_influence.png)](/Buccaneers "Buccaneers influence") **+0.1** The buccaneers influence
*   [![Marines force limit.png](/images/thumb/9/9f/Marines_force_limit.png/28px-Marines_force_limit.png)](/Marines_force_limit "Marines force limit") **+25%** Marines force limit
*   [![National sailors modifier.png](/images/thumb/3/33/National_sailors_modifier.png/28px-National_sailors_modifier.png)](/National_sailors_modifier "National sailors modifier") **+25%** National sailors modifier

![Expand Buccaneers' Power icon](/images/thumb/c/ce/Gov_sea_raiders.png/40px-Gov_sea_raiders.png "Expand Buccaneers' Power icon")

The Buccaneers are the backbone of our free harbor of pirates. Without them the loot of the wealthy merchants will not find its way into our chests. By expanding their leeway in what they can do, we can ensure a steady income of new loot.

**Conditions:**

*   Is [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

**Power to the Smugglers**

*   [![Smugglers influence](/images/thumb/5/5e/Smugglers_influence.png/28px-Smugglers_influence.png)](/Smugglers "Smugglers influence") **+0.1** The smugglers influence
*   [![Merchants.png](/images/thumb/2/24/Merchants.png/28px-Merchants.png)](/Merchant "Merchant") **+1** Merchant
*   [![Ship tradepower propagation.png](/images/thumb/b/b5/Ship_tradepower_propagation.png/28px-Ship_tradepower_propagation.png)](/Ship_tradepower_propagation "Ship tradepower propagation") **+25%** Ship tradepower propagation

![Power to the Smugglers icon](/images/thumb/8/81/Gov_blackmailing.png/40px-Gov_blackmailing.png "Power to the Smugglers icon")

Not all gold comes from lost treasures or from looted merchant ships. Some come from the trade with goods some might consider illegal. Of course legality is more like a suggestion to the Smugglers than a rule. By granting them additional power they will have an easier time infiltrating the markets.

**Conditions:**

*   Is [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

**Captains in Charge**

*   [![Captains influence](/images/thumb/c/cd/Captains_influence.png/28px-Captains_influence.png)](/Captains "Captains influence") **+0.1** Monthly captains influence
*   [![Heavy ship combat ability.png](/images/thumb/6/64/Heavy_ship_combat_ability.png/28px-Heavy_ship_combat_ability.png)](/Heavy_ship_combat_ability "Heavy ship combat ability") **+10%** Heavy ship combat ability
*   [![Fleet movement speed.png](/images/thumb/6/61/Fleet_movement_speed.png/28px-Fleet_movement_speed.png)](/Fleet_movement_speed "Fleet movement speed") **+1** Fleet movement speed

![Captains in Charge icon](/images/thumb/3/37/Gov_pirate_queen.png/40px-Gov_pirate_queen.png "Captains in Charge icon")

Let's face it: what is a Pirate without a ship? A petty thief at best. By putting our Captains in charge of the state we can get access to the finest ships this world has to offer.

**Conditions:**

*   Is [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

### Guiding Principle of Administration\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=16 "Edit section: Guiding Principle of Administration") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=16 "Edit section: Guiding Principle of Administration")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Political Principle**

*   [![Administrative possible policies.png](/images/thumb/e/e9/Administrative_possible_policies.png/28px-Administrative_possible_policies.png)](/Administrative_possible_policies "Administrative possible policies") **+1** Administrative possible policies

![Political Principle icon](/images/thumb/c/cf/Gov_paper_with_seal_3.png/40px-Gov_paper_with_seal_3.png "Political Principle icon")

As a Republic the guiding principles of our state must be those that further the efficiency of the political apparatus and the political ideals.

**Moral Principle**

*   [![Diplomatic possible policies.png](/images/thumb/b/b1/Diplomatic_possible_policies.png/28px-Diplomatic_possible_policies.png)](/Diplomatic_possible_policies "Diplomatic possible policies") **+1** Diplomatic possible policies

![Moral Principle icon](/images/thumb/b/b6/Gov_parliament_hall.png/40px-Gov_parliament_hall.png "Moral Principle icon")

One of the primary functions of the state is to uphold good and moral values. As our Republic in many ways relies on the good and virtuous behavior of its citizens corruption and sinful behavior must be counteracted and rooted out for the good of the entire country.

**Defense Principle**

*   [![Military possible policies.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Military_possible_policies.png/28px-Military_possible_policies.png)](/Military_possible_policies "Military possible policies") **+1** Military possible policies

![Defense Principle icon](/images/thumb/5/5a/Gov_soldiers_6.png/40px-Gov_soldiers_6.png "Defense Principle icon")

The highest principle of our republic is the protection of the people. Although it is not a popular topic in our government it is important to maintain a system of military for self-defense and maintenance of the internal stability.

**Principle of Enlightenment**

*   [![Years of separatism.png](/images/thumb/a/a2/Years_of_separatism.png/28px-Years_of_separatism.png)](/Years_of_separatism "Years of separatism") **−10** Years of separatism

![Principle of Enlightenment icon](/images/thumb/0/00/Gov_enlightenment.png/40px-Gov_enlightenment.png "Principle of Enlightenment icon")

The Enlightenment is the next intellectual and philosophical step of our society. To embrace the ideas of the Enlightenment is our principle so we can progress into a new era.

**Conditions:**

*   One of the following :
    *   Has completed [![Innovative idea group.png](/images/thumb/0/0d/Innovative_idea_group.png/28px-Innovative_idea_group.png)](/Innovative_ideas "Innovative ideas") Innovative Ideas
    *   The country has embraced the [![Enlightenment.png](/images/thumb/f/fa/Enlightenment.png/28px-Enlightenment.png)](/Enlightenment "Enlightenment") Enlightenment institution

**Military Principle**

*   [![Yearly republican tradition.png](/images/thumb/6/68/Yearly_republican_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_republican_tradition.png)](/Yearly_republican_tradition "Yearly republican tradition") **−0.5** Yearly republican tradition
*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism") **+10** Maximum absolutism
*   [![Years of separatism.png](/images/thumb/a/a2/Years_of_separatism.png/28px-Years_of_separatism.png)](/Years_of_separatism "Years of separatism") **−5** Years of separatism

![Military Principle icon](/images/thumb/7/75/Gov_soldiers_3.png/40px-Gov_soldiers_3.png "Military Principle icon")

The Republic is surrounded by enemies who seek the destruction of our state; the restoration of the monarchy. It is our utter most priority - our principle - to use our military might to expand the republic.

**Additional Effects:**

*   Winning wars gives **+5** [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") Republican Tradition (separate peaces do not count)

  

**Revolutionary Principle**

*   [![Morale of armies.png](/images/thumb/f/fa/Morale_of_armies.png/28px-Morale_of_armies.png)](/Morale_of_armies "Morale of armies") **+10%** Morale of armies
*   [![National manpower modifier.png](/images/thumb/f/fe/National_manpower_modifier.png/28px-National_manpower_modifier.png)](/National_manpower_modifier "National manpower modifier") **+15%** National manpower modifier
*    [![Girondist influence](/images/thumb/e/e9/Girondist_influence.png/28px-Girondist_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Girondist influence") **+0.1** Girondist influence

![Revolutionary Principle icon](/images/thumb/5/56/Gov_revolutionary_republic.png/40px-Gov_revolutionary_republic.png "Revolutionary Principle icon")

The purpose of our state is quite simple; to spread the Revolution. We must centralise our state around the idea that it is only be liberating all people of the world into Revolutionary states that we may create an everlasting state of peace and equality in the world.

**Conditions:**

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

Available only with the [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

*   Is [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target")revolutionary

  

**Equality Principle**

*   [![Tolerance heretic.png](/images/thumb/2/27/Tolerance_heretic.png/28px-Tolerance_heretic.png)](/Tolerance_of_heretics "Tolerance of heretics") **+2** Tolerance of heretics
*   [![Tolerance heathen.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Tolerance_heathen.png/28px-Tolerance_heathen.png)](/Tolerance_of_heathens "Tolerance of heathens") **+2** Tolerance of heathens
*    [![Jacobin influence](/images/thumb/4/4e/Jacobin_influence.png/28px-Jacobin_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Jacobin influence") **+0.1** Jacobin influence

![Equality Principle icon](/images/thumb/f/fb/Reform_equal_electorate.png/40px-Reform_equal_electorate.png "Equality Principle icon")

Although our state holds Egalité as one of its core values, it is clear that we have completely failed in our goal to treat all our people with fairness and equality. The core principle of our nation must be to eliminate the barriers of gender, culture, and social class and ensure that it is known that all people are created equal and a good start to that would be to ensure that religion remains a private matter and does not dictate one’s rights within the state.

**Conditions:**

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

Available only with the [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

*   Is [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target")revolutionary

  

**Imperial Principle**

*   [![Aggressive expansion impact.png](/images/thumb/c/ca/Aggressive_expansion_impact.png/28px-Aggressive_expansion_impact.png)](/Aggressive_expansion_impact "Aggressive expansion impact") **−10%** Aggressive expansion impact
*   [![Province war score cost.png](/images/thumb/9/9c/Province_war_score_cost.png/28px-Province_war_score_cost.png)](/Province_war_score_cost "Province war score cost") **−10%** Province war score cost
*    [![Imperial influence](/images/thumb/5/5b/Imperial_influence.png/28px-Imperial_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Imperial influence") **+0.1** Imperial influence

![Imperial Principle icon](/images/thumb/8/8f/Reform_imperial_nobility.png/40px-Reform_imperial_nobility.png "Imperial Principle icon")

The Revolution has made it clear that our nation, above all others, wields the divine right to hold Imperial Hegemony over all other nations. The states around us are fragile and weak, and it is clear that only by directly controlling these states ourselves will we ensure that the values of the Revolution are enforced on the people.

**Conditions:**

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

Available only with the [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

*   Is [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target")revolutionary

  

### Electorate\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=17 "Edit section: Electorate") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=17 "Edit section: Electorate")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Landholders**

*   [![Manpower recovery speed.png](/images/thumb/e/ee/Manpower_recovery_speed.png/28px-Manpower_recovery_speed.png)](/Manpower_recovery "Manpower recovery") **+10%** Manpower recovery speed

![Landholders icon](/images/thumb/8/8a/Gov_dutch_flag.png/40px-Gov_dutch_flag.png "Landholders icon")

The landholders are at the heart of power in any society and our state is no exception. Let us extend the power to vote to all those that have land and grade their number of votes in accordance with the size of their properties.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary

**Citizenry**

*   [![Morale of armies.png](/images/thumb/f/fa/Morale_of_armies.png/28px-Morale_of_armies.png)](/Morale_of_armies "Morale of armies") **+10%** Morale of armies

![Citizenry icon](/images/thumb/0/05/Gov_people_walking.png/40px-Gov_people_walking.png "Citizenry icon")

A Republic relies on its citizens to function and so it is only right that each citizen in our state will have the power to vote for who will guide our country. Attaining the privilege of being a citizen will also be a spur for all those under our rule to strive for good conduct.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary

![Dynastic Rule icon](/images/thumb/4/49/Gov_king.png/40px-Gov_king.png "Dynastic Rule icon")

Connections are more powerful than any sword could ever be. Through the installment of a dynasty as the political head of the state it is possible for us to build diplomatic relations with monarchies while still maintaining the principles of the republic.That the elected ruler seems to be a member of the same family is just a pure coincidence.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary

*   Ruler reigns for life. No elections.

**Board of Admirals**

*   [![Naval leader fire.png](/images/thumb/4/41/Naval_leader_fire.png/28px-Naval_leader_fire.png)](/Naval_leader_fire "Naval leader fire") **+1** Naval leader fire
*   [![Yearly republican tradition.png](/images/thumb/6/68/Yearly_republican_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_republican_tradition.png)](/Yearly_republican_tradition "Yearly republican tradition") **−0.5** Yearly republican tradition

*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism")**+10** Maximum Absolutism

![Board of Admirals icon](/images/thumb/0/01/Reform_admiralty.png/40px-Reform_admiralty.png "Board of Admirals icon")

Our nation lives and dies on our ability to project power on the sea. To that end we have handed over the reins of government to the Board of Admirals, whose members are experienced and patriotic beyond reproach.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary
*   _Not_ available for ‘Pirate Republics’ or ‘Dutch Republic’
*   Has a port in the capital state

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   Ruler reigns for life. No elections.
*   Cannot fall under a Presidential Dictatorship
*   ‘An [![Admiral.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Admiral.png/28px-Admiral.png)](/Admiral "Admiral") Admiral becomes ruler when the current ruler dies.’
*   Ruler stats depend on [![Admiral.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Admiral.png/28px-Admiral.png)](/Admiral "Admiral") admiral pips. On average 12 ruler points for 16-pips admiral.

**Military Rulership**

*   [![Land leader shock.png](/images/thumb/4/4c/Land_leader_shock.png/28px-Land_leader_shock.png)](/Land_leader_shock "Land leader shock") **+1** Land leader shock
*   [![Yearly army tradition.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Yearly_army_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_army_tradition.png)](/Yearly_army_tradition "Yearly army tradition") **+0.5** Yearly army tradition

*   [![Maximum absolutism](/images/thumb/a/aa/Maximum_absolutism.png/28px-Maximum_absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Maximum absolutism") **+10** Maximum absolutism

![Military Rulership icon](/images/thumb/c/cb/Gov_soldiers_2.png/40px-Gov_soldiers_2.png "Military Rulership icon")

The republic is a thorn in the side for many potential enemies who seek to destroy us. For the sake of the country's safety we granted the generals the reins of our government. May their experience and love to their home country protect the republic. \\n\\nDisables elections.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary

*   Ruler reigns for life. No elections.

**Equal Electorate**

*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/Unrest "Unrest") **−2** National unrest
*   [![National tax modifier.png](/images/thumb/3/34/National_tax_modifier.png/28px-National_tax_modifier.png)](/National_tax_modifier "National tax modifier") **+10%** National tax modifier

*   [![Jacobin influence](/images/thumb/4/4e/Jacobin_influence.png/28px-Jacobin_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Jacobin influence") **+0.1** Jacobin influence

![Equal Electorate icon](/images/thumb/f/fb/Reform_equal_electorate.png/40px-Reform_equal_electorate.png "Equal Electorate icon")

We must dissolve all barriers that separate our people and extend the right to hold a political office to all people. Gender, religion, social class, culture, all are irrelevant to one’s capability to hold a political office and so we must strive to maintain equality of opportunity within our government.

**Conditions:**

*   Only available for [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary countries with the [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

**Three Social Classes**

*   [![Core-creation cost.png](/images/thumb/5/56/Core-creation_cost.png/28px-Core-creation_cost.png)](/Core-creation_cost "Core-creation cost") **−10%** Core-creation cost
*   [![Girondist influence](/images/thumb/e/e9/Girondist_influence.png/28px-Girondist_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Girondist influence") **+0.1** Girondist influence

![Three Social Classes icon](/images/thumb/c/cb/Reform_three_classes.png/40px-Reform_three_classes.png "Three Social Classes icon")

In the days before the birth of the Revolution, the old government attempted to sway the people away from taking arms by allowing three social classes representation within the government; the clergy, the peasants, and the upper class. Perhaps we could emulate this system by organizing our people into an upper, middle, and lower class based on their economic status and creating three distinct political entities within our government to represent their interests.

**Conditions:**

*   Only available for [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") revolutionary countries with the [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

  

**Military Electorate**

*   [![Yearly army tradition.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Yearly_army_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_army_tradition.png)](/Yearly_army_tradition "Yearly army tradition") **+0.25** Yearly army tradition
*   [![Land leader fire.png](/images/thumb/2/27/Land_leader_fire.png/28px-Land_leader_fire.png)](/Land_leader_fire "Land leader fire") **+1** Land leader fire
*    [![Imperial influence](/images/thumb/5/5b/Imperial_influence.png/28px-Imperial_influence.png)](/Revolutionary_republic "Imperial influence") **+0.1** Imperial influence

![Military Electorate icon](/images/thumb/8/8a/Reform_military_dictatorship.png/40px-Reform_military_dictatorship.png "Military Electorate icon")

Our nation values comradery above all else, and nobody exemplifies the value of being a comrade like our boys fighting on the fields of battle. These are the men who’ve seen the horrors of war and fought alongside their countrymen to preserve and advance the Revolution, and these men should be the ones to rule us. We must alter the requirements to hold an office in our government so that only those who have served in our military are eligible to represent the people within the government.

**Conditions:**

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

Available only with the [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

*   Is [![Revolution target.png](/images/thumb/8/8a/Revolution_target.png/28px-Revolution_target.png)](/Revolution_target "Revolution target")revolutionary

* * *

**Additional effects:**

*   A [![General.png](/images/thumb/6/6d/General.png/28px-General.png)](/General "General") [general](/General "General") becomes ruler when the current ruler dies.
*   Ruler reigns for life. No elections.
*   Mutually exclusive with [The Feuillant System](/Republic#The_Feuillant_System "Republic")

  

**Rule through Loot**

*   [![Looting speed.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Looting_speed.png/28px-Looting_speed.png)](/Looting_speed "Looting speed") **+100%** Looting speed
*   [![Land attrition.png](/images/thumb/d/df/Land_attrition.png/28px-Land_attrition.png)](/Land_attrition "Land attrition") **−5%** Land attrition

![Rule through Loot icon](/images/thumb/c/ce/Gov_rioting_burning_2.png/40px-Gov_rioting_burning_2.png "Rule through Loot icon")

We live in a world where no one trusts anybody and the only way to hold any kind of power is by promises of loot. Fortunately, our kind understands this rule.

**Conditions:**

*   Is [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

### Office Selection\[[edit](/index.php?title=Republic&veaction=edit&section=18 "Edit section: Office Selection") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Republic&action=edit&section=18 "Edit section: Office Selection")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Appointment by Committee**

*   [![Advisor cost.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Advisor_cost.png/28px-Advisor_cost.png)](/Advisor_costs "Advisor costs") **−5%** Advisor costs
*   [![Possible advisors.png](/images/thumb/4/42/Possible_advisors.png/28px-Possible_advisors.png)](/Possible_advisors "Possible advisors") **+1** Possible advisor

![Appointment by Committee icon](/images/thumb/6/61/Gov_politician.png/40px-Gov_politician.png "Appointment by Committee icon")

Let us abandon arbitrary appointments to governmental offices. Committees shall be established to decide on the best candidate for a given role to ensure that administrative competence is the norm in our realm.

**Bureaucratic Aparatus**

*   [![Minimum autonomy in territories.png](/images/thumb/4/44/Minimum_autonomy_in_territories.png/28px-Minimum_autonomy_in_territories.png)](/Minimum_autonomy "Minimum autonomy") **−10%** Minimum autonomy in territories

**Extended Suffrage**

*   [![Diplomatic free policies.png](/images/thumb/b/b6/Diplomatic_free_policies.png/28px-Diplomatic_free_policies.png)](/Diplomatic_free_policies "Diplomatic free policies") **+1** Diplomatic free policies

![Extended Suffrage icon](/images/thumb/9/93/Gov_paper_with_seal.png/40px-Gov_paper_with_seal.png "Extended Suffrage icon")

Let us open up the availability of important offices to more of those living within our borders so that we have a wider and more representative selection of civil servants.

**Pirate Council**

*   [![Yearly republican tradition.png](/images/thumb/6/68/Yearly_republican_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_republican_tradition.png)](/Yearly_republican_tradition "Yearly republican tradition") **+0.5** Yearly republican tradition

![Pirate Council icon](/images/thumb/0/07/Gov_council.png/40px-Gov_council.png "Pirate Council icon")

We might live and operate outside any imperial law, but we are not an unorganized, backstabbing group of criminals. Every free port of our confederation is seat to an influential captain. These captains make the Pirate Council which ensures that the internal rules of the confederation are honored.

**Conditions:**

*   Is [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’
